HTTP filters are registered using REGISTER_FACTORY macro that creates instances of NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory subclasses\n2. During configuration parsing in FilterChainHelper::processFilters, the factory is retrieved from the registry and createFilterFactoryFromProto is called to get a FilterFactoryCb (a callback)\n3. These callbacks are stored in FilterFactoriesList and passed to FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories\n4. For each stream/request, FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb is called with the stored callbacks\n\n\n5. The `processFilter()` method:\\n\\n1. Retrieves the factory from the registry using `Config::Utility::getAndCheckFactory<NeutralNamedHttpFilterFactory>()`\\n2. Calls `factory->createFilterFactoryFromProto()` to obtain a `FilterFactoryCb` callback\\n3. Wraps the callback in a **FilterConfigProviderPtr** and stores it in a **FilterFactoriesList**\\n\\nFor dynamic filters, the **HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl** in `source/common/filter/config_discovery_impl.h` handles runtime filter instantiation via `instantiateFilterFactory()`, which also calls the factory's `createFilterFactoryFromProto()` method.\\n\\n## Filter Chain Creation for Factories\\n\\nThe **FilterChainUtility::createFilterChainForFactories()** function in `source/common/http/filter_chain_helper.cc` iterates through stored filter factories and calls `manager.applyFilterFactoryCb()` for each one, passing the factory's callback.\\n\\n## Per-Request Filter Instantiation\\n\\nWhen a new HTTP stream is created, the **FilterManager** in `source/common/http/filter_manager.h` calls `applyFilterFactoryCb()` (implemented in `source/common/http/filter_manager.cc` at line 551):\\n\\n```cpp\\nvoid FilterManager::applyFilterFactoryCb(FilterContext context, FilterFactoryCb& factory) {\\n  FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl callbacks(*this, context);\\n  factory(callbacks);\\n}\\n```\\n\\nThis invokes the stored callback with a **FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl** object, which implements **Http::FilterChainFactoryCallbacks**. The actual filter instances are created when the callback calls methods like:\\n\\n- `addStreamDecoderFilter()` - adds decoder-only filters\\n- `addStreamEncoderFilter()` - adds encoder-only filters  \\n- `addStreamFilter()` - adds dual encoder/decoder filters\\n\\nThese methods (lines 918-938 in filter_manager.h) wrap the filter instances in **ActiveStreamDecoderFilter** and **ActiveStreamEncoderFilter** objects, which manage the filter's lifecycle, iteration state, and data processing on the request/response paths.\\n\\n## Key Components\\n\\n- **NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory**: Interface for filter factories, registered in the global registry\\n- **FilterChainHelper**: Processes static filter configs during HCM initialization\\n- **HttpDynamicFilterConfigProviderImpl**: Provides runtime filter instantiation via xDS\\n- **FilterManager**: Manages per-stream filter chains and execution\\n- **FilterChainFactoryCallbacksImpl**: Bridge between factory callbacks and actual filter creation\\n- **ActiveStreamDecoderFilter/EncoderFilter**: Wrappers for filter instances that handle iteration and state management\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
